Abstract: We investigate the luminosity-temperature ($L$-$T$) relation of galaxy clusters as a probe for testing modified gravity (MG) theories, focusing on $f(R)$ gravity and symmetron models. Using an improved semi-analytic framework that incorporates angular momentum acquisition, dynamical friction, and shock heating within the modified punctuated equilibrium model, we compare predictions against hydrodynamical simulations and observational data. While massive clusters remain largely screened and follow standard $Λ$CDM predictions, low-mass systems ($kT \lesssim 1-2$ keV) exhibit systematic deviations characterized by steeper $L$-$T$ slopes in MG scenarios. Crucially, we demonstrate that these signatures cannot be mimicked by conventional astrophysical processes such as feedback or angular momentum effects, which primarily affect normalization rather than curvature. Our results establish the $L$-$T$ relation as a robust diagnostic tool for distinguishing general relativity from screened MG theories, with the strongest discriminatory power emerging at group scales accessible to current and future X-ray surveys. Moreover, a normalized reduced $χ^2$ analysis of the $L$-$T$ relation shows that MG models provide significantly better agreement with observational data than $Λ$CDM, with several realizations achieving excellent fits while the $Λ$CDM model consistently performs worst.

### [119] [Calibrating spectral siren cosmology with synthetic catalogs of binary black hole mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15332)
*Arianna Scarpa,Simone Mastrogiovanni,Filippo Santoliquido,Manuel Arca-Sedda*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于标准化流（Normalizing Flows）的双黑洞（BBH）种群建模方法，用于校准引力波标准汽笛的红移，从而更准确地测定哈勃常数 H₀；在 GWTC-4.0 数据上测得 H₀ = 71.62⁺⁴·⁰⁴₋₄·₀₀ km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹，并揭示 H₀ 与 BBH 形成通道（孤立演化 vs 动力学形成）比例存在简并。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双黑洞并合作为标准汽笛可直接提供光度距离，但其红移与源质量简并；传统质量谱建模误差会显著偏置哈勃常数 H₀ 的测量，亟需更稳健的种群建模方法。

Method: 构建基于标准化流的 BBH 种群模型，训练于包含孤立演化和动力学形成通道的天体物理合成星表；用模拟数据验证模型对真实分布的重建能力，并应用于 GWTC-4.0 实际引力波数据进行 H₀ 推断。

Result: 模型在模拟数据中成功消除 H₀ 系统偏差；在 GWTC-4.0 上得到 H₀ = 71.62⁺⁴·⁰⁴₋₄·₀₀ km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹；发现 H₀ 推断与动力学通道占比存在简并：Planck 宇宙学偏好约 35%，SH0ES 偏好约 25%。

Conclusion: 标准化流模型能有效缓解 BBH 质量谱误设导致的 H₀ 偏差，提升标准汽笛宇宙学精度；同时揭示了恒星演化模型参数与宇宙学参数之间的内在关联，为多信使宇宙学提供新约束路径。

Abstract: Binary black hole (BBH) mergers detected through Gravitational Waves (GWs) are a promising probe for the cosmic expansion. These sources are standard sirens for which we can directly measure the luminosity distance, but their redshift is degenerate with the determination of their source masses. In analogy to standard candles, the redshift of standard sirens can be obtained using a calibration based on the source mass spectrum, but without the need for a cosmological ladder. It has been recently shown that a mismodeling of the BBH mass spectrum is very likely to introduce a bias in the determination of the Hubble constant. To tackle this issue, we develop a BBH population model based on Normalizing Flows, trained on synthetic BBH catalogs generated from astrophysical prescriptions, including binaries formed through both isolated stellar evolution and dynamical environments. We validate this approach with a mock BBH dataset, demonstrating that the Normalizing Flow framework faithfully recovers the true distribution and eliminates systematic biases in the Hubble constant inference. By using this model on GWTC-4.0 data, we obtain $H_0 = 71.62^{+4.04}_{-4.00}\; km \; s^{-1} Mpc^{-1}$ at 68.3% credible interval. Assuming the astrophysical prescriptions present in B-POP, we also show that the determination of $H_0$ is degenerate with the fraction of binaries born in the dynamical and isolated formation channel, with a Planck cosmology favouring $\sim 35\%$ binaries formed in the dynamical environment while a SH0ES cosmology favouring a value of $\sim 25\%$.

### [120] [Wasserstein Distance in Cosmological Structure Formation: An Optimal Transport Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15342)
*Tsutomu T. Takeuchi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文将宇宙大尺度结构形成建模为质量分布的最优传输问题，利用Wasserstein距离统一刻画引力演化、星系形成偏置和采样噪声三类物理过程，并提出其作为连接连续密度场与离散星系巡天的新统计量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统统计量（如功率谱、相关函数）仅描述密度涨落的幅度结构，无法直接刻画结构形成中物质的空间再分布过程。

Method: 基于最优传输理论，将从初始线性密度场到观测星系样本的生成过程建模为连续密度场到点过程的分层映射，并在小涨落近似下推导出二者间Wasserstein距离的近似表达式。

Result: Wasserstein距离可自然分解为三部分：引力导致的质量输运项（正比于物质功率谱积分）、星系形成偏置项（加权星系相关函数积分）和星系离散采样引起的泊松散粒噪声项。

Conclusion: Wasserstein距离为宇宙大尺度结构形成提供了基于传输几何的统一描述框架，有望成为连接理论密度场与观测星系巡天的新统计工具。

Abstract: The formation of cosmological large-scale structure is usually described in terms of the evolution of density fluctuations and their statistical measures, such as the power spectrum and correlation function. However, these statistics characterize the amplitude structure of density fluctuations and do not directly describe the spatial redistribution of matter that occurs during structure formation. In this work we formulate cosmological structure formation as a transport problem of mass distributions using the Wasserstein distance from optimal transport theory. The generative process from the initial linear density field to the observed galaxy catalog is treated as a hierarchical mapping from a continuous density field to a galaxy point process, and an approximate expression for the Wasserstein distance between them is derived under the small-fluctuation approximation. We show that this distance naturally decomposes into contributions associated with three physical processes: mass transport by gravitational evolution, galaxy formation bias, and shot noise arising from the discrete sampling of galaxies. The gravitational transport term is expressed as an integral of the matter power spectrum, while the galaxy formation contribution appears as a weighted integral of the galaxy correlation function. The sampling term corresponds to Poisson shot noise originating from the discreteness of the galaxy catalog. These results provide a unified framework for describing cosmological large-scale structure formation from the perspective of transport geometry and suggest that the Wasserstein distance may serve as a new statistical quantity linking continuous density fields with observed galaxy catalogs.

</details>


### [121] [When One-Parameter Dark Energy Makes Neutrinos Physical Again](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15422)
*Weiqiang Yang,Eleonora Di Valentino,Eric V. Linder,Sibo Zhang,Supriya Pan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了不同暗能量状态方程（DE EoS）对中微子质量符号的影响，发现某些单参数DE EoS（特别是高红移为幻影型、低红移穿越w=-1）足以使中微子质量后验分布回到正值，无需双参数模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前ΛCDM模型下宇宙学数据倾向于负的中微子质量和，这与物理常识矛盾；需探究何种暗能量模型能缓解该问题。

Method: 系统比较多种具物理意义的单参数暗能量状态方程（如w(z)模型），分析其对中微子质量后验分布的影响，并与wCDM和w0waCDM模型对比。

Result: 某些单参数DE EoS（如高红移w<-1、低红移穿越w=-1的模型）可使中微子质量后验显著回归正值，效果接近w0waCDM；而常数wCDM无效。

Conclusion: 数据倾向特定物理性质（高红移幻影行为+穿越w=-1），而非泛泛的参数简并；单参数模型已足够解释中微子质量符号问题。

Abstract: A puzzling implication of current data interpreted in the $Λ$CDM cosmology is the preference for a negative sum of neutrino masses. Moving to $w_0w_a$CDM brings an appreciable fraction of the neutrino mass posterior back to positive values, while the constant equation-of-state dark energy case $w$CDM does not. We investigate a variety of one-parameter dark energy equations of state (DE EoS), each variation with particular physical properties, to understand whether a two-parameter DE EoS is required to bring the neutrino mass positive. The conclusion is that certain one-parameter DE EoS can suffice, implying that the data are pointing toward physical characteristics rather than a broad degeneracy. The required characteristics are identified as phantom dark energy at high redshift, crossing $w=-1$ at lower redshift.

### [122] [Probing Gravitational-Wave Four-Point Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15514)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机引力波背景（SGWB）是探测早期宇宙物理和暗区动力学的重要工具，但目前大多数研究仅关注其功率谱，而更高阶关联器中蕴含更多统计信息。

Method: 在矢量涨落二次产生SGWB的框架下，发展了刻画高阶引力波关联器的工具，并计算了对引力波四谱有连通贡献的代表性四点函数；分析了其对重叠约化函数方差的影响，并构建了地面干涉仪测量连通四谱的最优估计量。

Result: 发现四谱振幅正比于引力波功率谱的平方，并在折叠动量构型处达到峰值；连通四谱会影响两点重叠约化函数（如Hellings-Downs曲线）的方差；提出了地面干涉仪测量该信号的最优估计方法。

Conclusion: SGWB的非高斯统计特性可作为补充观测量，有助于揭示引力波背景起源，并区分宇宙学与天体物理来源。

Abstract: Stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds (SGWBs) of primordial origin offer a powerful probe of early-Universe physics and possible dark-sector dynamics. While most searches focus on the GW power spectrum, additional information is encoded in higher-order correlators that characterize the statistical properties of the signal. In this work we study non-Gaussian features of a cosmological SGWB generated at second order by vector fluctuations, a class of sources well motivated in early-Universe scenarios. Within this framework we develop tools to characterize higher-order GW correlators and compute representative four-point functions that generate a connected contribution to the GW trispectrum. We show that the trispectrum amplitude scales as the square of the GW power spectrum and peaks in characteristic folded momentum configurations, reflecting the structure of the nonlinear source. We then explore the observational implications. First, we demonstrate that the connected trispectrum contributes to the variance of two-point overlap reduction functions, including the Hellings-Downs curve relevant for pulsar timing arrays. We then construct the optimal estimator to measure the connected trispectrum with ground-based interferometers. Our results highlight how non-Gaussian SGWB statistics provide a complementary observable to probe the origin of GW backgrounds and to distinguish cosmological from astrophysical sources.

### [123] [A Hybrid Framework for Kilonova Anomaly Detection using Single-Epoch SEDs from the 7-Dimensional Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13814)
*Gregory S. H. Paek,Myungshin Im,Seo-Won Chang,Hyeonho Choi,Ji Hoon Kim*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合无监督异常检测（Isolation Forest）与有监督多分类（XGBoost）的混合框架，利用7维望远镜（7DT）单历元中波段测光数据高效识别千新星（KNe），在模拟数据上实现高召回率（>90%）与高分类精度（macro F1 ~0.82），并揭示关键滤光片贡献，支持实时引力波后随与巡天预警应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为应对引力波事件后快速、可靠识别光学对应体（如千新星）的需求，以及现有瞬变源分类器对罕见、未训练目标（如KNe）泛化能力不足的问题，需发展不依赖KNe标注样本、仅基于常规瞬变模拟即可触发高置信度异常警报的新方法。

Method: 构建双阶段混合分类框架：第一阶段用Isolation Forest对单历元7DT中波段SED进行无监督异常检测；第二阶段用XGBoost对八类常见瞬变（Ia/Ibc/II型超新星、SLSNe、TDEs、AGN、变星、小行星）进行有监督多分类；训练数据基于考虑各滤光片灵敏度的真实感7DT测光模拟；采用SHAP分析滤光片重要性，并评估子集滤光片组合性能。

Result: XGBoost在40个滤光片下达到macro F1≈0.82；Isolation Forest无需KNe训练即召回>90%模拟及已知KNe（AT 2017gfo），污染率低；SHAP分析表明仅需40–50%最有效滤光片即可维持基线性能，红端滤光片贡献微弱；40个7DT滤光片的前半+单个LSST波段可复现全模型精度（误差1–2%）。

Conclusion: 7DT中波段系统配合该混合框架，可在单历元数据下实现高精度、高可解释性瞬变分类与异常探测，适用于GW后随观测、Rubin警报流过滤及7DT巡天中的偶然瞬变发现。

Abstract: We develop a hybrid framework to identify kilonovae (KNe), using single-epoch, medium-band spectral energy distributions from the 7-Dimensional Telescope (7DT). The framework integrates an unsupervised anomaly classifier (\texttt{Isolation Forest}) to flag unusual events with a supervised multi-class classifier (\texttt{XGBoost}) that characterizes eight common transient types. Trained on realistically simulated 7DT photometry accounting for per-filter sensitivity, the classifier achieves macro $F_{1}\sim0.80$ ($\sim0.82$) with 20 (40) filters across eight classes, Type~Ia/Ibc/II SNe, SLSNe, TDEs, AGN, stellar variables, and asteroids. Without direct training, the anomaly detector recovers $>$90\% of simulated and observed optically detectable KNe (AT~2017gfo) with a low contamination fraction, with a caveat of limitations of the training sample such as limited redshift range of SNe ($z < 0.15$), and a relatively small number of early non-KNe spectra. A SHAP-based feature analysis reveals that only $\sim$40--50\% of the most informative filters are sufficient to retain near-baseline performance, while red-end filters contribute little. Combining the top-ranked half of the 40 7DT filters with a single LSST band reproduces the full-model accuracy within 1--2\%, suggesting practical follow-up strategies. These results demonstrate that 7DT's medium-band system enables rapid, interpretable classifications and reliable anomaly alerts from single-epoch data -- promising for gravitational-wave follow-up, Rubin alert stream filtering, and serendipitous transient discovery in the 7DT survey.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 最终紧凑模型F1-score≈0.844，PR-AUC≈0.928；时间演化特征主导分类能力，亮度、颜色和变异性特征起辅助作用；约10个核心物理特征即可保留近全部性能。

Abstract: Photometric classification of Type Ia supernovae is essential for modern time-domain surveys, where spectroscopic confirmation is not always feasible for the full transient sample. In this work, we investigate a compact and physically interpretable feature representation derived from multi-band light curves and evaluate its performance using gradient-boosted decision trees on the Supernova Photometric Classification Challenge (SPCC) dataset. Starting from a reduced 16-feature model, we perform a systematic feature ablation study to determine which physical descriptors contribute most strongly to classification performance. The final compact model achieves an F1-score of approximately 0.844 and a precision--recall area under the curve (PR-AUC) of approximately 0.928. The ablation results show that temporal evolution provides the dominant classification signal, while brightness, color, and variability features supply complementary information. A reduced core of approximately ten physically meaningful features retains nearly the full performance of the compact model, indicating that reliable classification does not require large high-dimensional feature spaces. These results show that interpretable feature-based models can capture the essential astrophysical information needed for Type Ia photometric classification, with direct implications for survey cadence, filter coverage, and the design of transparent machine learning pipelines for future time-domain surveys.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用非传统光学设计与新型信号编码架构，在16U立方星平台上实现窄角天体测量，通过监测双星轨道的引力摄动来间接探测系外行星。

Abstract: The TOLIMAN project is engaged with the construction, launch and operation of a low-cost space telescope of unorthodox optical design. Its primary science goal targets an exhaustive search for temperate-orbit rocky planets around either star in the alpha Centauri AB binary within our nearest-neighbor star system. Despite their favorable proximity and brightness, the detection of terrestrial exoplanets around such nearby Sun-like stars remains problematic for contemporary instrumental approaches. By performing narrow-angle astrometric monitoring of binary stars at extreme precision, any exoplanets will betray their presence by way of gravitationally-induced perturbations on the binary orbit. Recovery of this signal is challenging for it amounts to only a few microarcseconds of angular deflection (at best), and so is normally thought to require a large (meter-class) instrument. By implementing an innovative optical and signal encoding architecture, the TOLIMAN space telescope aims to recover such signals with a telescope aperture of only 12.5cm. This paper gives an overview of key features of the mission; in particular the concepts underlying the optics to enable image registration at the extreme levels of precision required. An outline is also provided, sketching further mission components and systems incorporated into the 16U CubeSat spacecraft bus in which the science payload is housed - all of which are now under construction.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建基于物理机制的电路模型（如校准源）；融合频率域拟合（卷积代价函数）与贝叶斯推断；利用实验室测量后验更新先验，实现迭代建模、鲁棒参数估计与不确定性量化。

Conclusion: 该框架可动态补偿系统非理想性随时间的漂移，为高精度全球21 cm观测提供了可扩展、可量化的校准新范式。

Abstract: Recent experiments in cosmology, particularly those aimed at detecting the faint, redshifted, global 21 cm hydrogen line (depth < ~200 mK, z > 7.5), have imposed stringent new requirements on radiometer calibration. In this work, we present a framework for circuit modeling and parameter inference to strengthen these calibration pipelines. This new approach enables in situ characterization of otherwise immeasurable systematics using physically motivated models. A combination of frequentist and Bayesian techniques are employed in a pipeline that supports iterative modeling, robust parameter estimation, and detailed uncertainty quantification. The framework is applied to the REACH telescope, where the precise correction of variations in the radio signal paths arising from component aging or environmental effects is critical. Circuit models of REACH's calibration sources are developed, with the goal of predicting source temperature corrections that are conventionally obtained from laboratory measurements. By fitting the models to measured data using a convolutional cost function, a strong agreement with RMS residuals no worse than -37 dB is obtained. However, Bayesian inference reveals that the resulting temperature corrections can have uncertainties on the order of 1 to 2 K, caused by reflection coefficient degeneracies, measurement noise, and errors in the models. To combat this, posteriors obtained from laboratory measurements are employed as updated priors, reducing correction uncertainties down to 75 mK. Ultimately, the framework provides a means of dynamically accounting for drift in system non-idealities over time, addressing the increasing precision demands of global 21 cm radio astronomy.

This paper discusses considerations for designing such hybrid data/metadata formats, and reviews some examples such as VOParquet, FITS-plus and ECSV. We focus on tabular data, but some of the considerations may apply to other datatypes such as arrays as well.

### [128] [A numerical framework for Newtonian-noise estimation at the Einstein Telescope: 2-D simulations beyond the plane-wave approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15424)
*Patrick Schillings,Shi Yao,Johannes Erdmann,Andreas Rietbrock*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于谱元法的数值框架，用于更精确地估计爱因斯坦望远镜（ET）中的牛顿噪声，尤其在1.7–6 Hz低频段；通过二维均匀介质验证了其与解析解的一致性，并用30个随机表面源模拟环境地震激发，发现P波比例低于常规假设，有利于噪声抑制；该框架可扩展至三维及复杂地质建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有牛顿噪声估算多依赖于忽略地质异质性和复杂波相互作用的解析或半解析模型，难以准确预测第三代引力波探测器爱因斯坦望远镜在低频段（1.7–6 Hz）受牛顿噪声限制的真实性能。

Method: 基于谱元法对地震波场进行数值模拟，构建牛顿噪声估算框架；首先在二维均匀介质中用单表面源与解析平面波解对比验证；再扩展至30个随机表面源以模拟稳态环境地震激发。

Result: 数值结果与解析解高度一致；在简单均匀模型下，模拟得到的P波比例显著低于通常假设值，表明牛顿噪声可能更容易被抑制；框架具备向三维、实测地质结构和地形集成的可行性。

Conclusion: 所提出的数值框架为爱因斯坦望远镜等未来地下引力波探测器提供了高保真、可推广的站点特异性牛顿噪声评估工具，有望提升低频灵敏度建模与减噪策略设计的准确性。

Abstract: The Einstein Telescope (ET) is a third-generation underground gravitational-wave observatory designed to extend the detection sensitivity down to a few Hertz. Newtonian noise is expected to limit the low-frequency sensitivity of ET, particularly in the 1.7-6 Hz band. Most existing estimates rely on analytical or semi-analytical models assuming homogeneous or layered media, neglecting geological heterogeneity and complex wave interactions. In this work, we present a numerical framework for Newtonian-noise estimation based on spectral-element simulations of a seismic wave field. As a proof of concept, we first benchmark the numerical results against analytical plane-wave predictions in a two-dimensional homogeneous medium with a single surface source, demonstrating excellent agreement for both bulk and cavern contributions. We then extend the model to an array of 30 stochastic surface sources to approximate stationary ambient seismic excitation. The P-wave fraction inferred from the simulated wave field is, in this simple homogeneous case, significantly lower than commonly assumed, indicating enhanced prospects for Newtonian-noise mitigation. The framework is readily applicable to three-dimensional simulations and to integration of detailed local seismic models and topography, offering strong potential for site-specific Newtonian-noise estimation.

### [129] [A flexible method for estimating luminosity functions via Kernel Density Estimation - III. Extending to Multiple Flux-Limited Samples](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15441)
*Zunli Yuan,Chuanqi Li,Wenjie Wang,Luozhenhan Liu*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于多通量限制样本的光度函数（LF）核密度估计（KDE）新框架，通过在光度-红移平面上按子样本通量限分段，并在各段内使用对应局部通量阈值作为截断边界进行变换-反射KDE，从而充分利用所有数据并保持统计一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往方法仅适用于单个通量限制样本，而实际巡天常包含多个观测深度和通量限不同的天区，需推广至多样本情形。

Method: 提出分段估计框架：将光度-红移平面按各子样本的阶梯状通量限划分为互斥区域；在每区域内整合所有能探测到该区域源的巡天数据，并以对应局部通量阈值为截断边界，应用变换-反射KDE方法。

Result: 蒙特卡洛模拟验证了方法的稳健性；应用于SDSS DR7与2SLAQ类星体数据时，通量限交界处过渡平滑，且与参数化模型高度一致。

Conclusion: 该方法可有效处理多通量限制样本，兼顾数据利用率与统计严谨性，并已集成于开源Python包kdeLF中。

Abstract: As the third paper in a series regarding the estimation of luminosity functions (LFs) via kernel density estimation (KDE), we present a further generalization of our framework by extending its applicability to multiple flux-limited samples. While our previous works addressed single flux-limited datasets, many practical surveys collect data from several disjoint sky regions with varying observational depths and flux limits. We introduce a piecewise estimation framework that partitions the luminosity-redshift plane into disjoint regions according to the staggered flux limits of the sub-samples. Within each region, we integrate data from all surveys capable of detecting sources into a combined sample and apply the transformation-reflection KDE method using the corresponding local flux threshold as the truncation boundary. This strategy allows for the full utilization of all available sources while maintaining rigorous statistical consistency. The robustness of this approach is validated through Monte Carlo simulations. Furthermore, application to SDSS DR7 and 2SLAQ quasar data shows smooth transitions across flux limits and excellent agreement with parametric models. This approach is fully supported by our previously developed \texttt{kdeLF} Python package.

</details>


### [130] [The Effect of "Roll-Drift" in ACS/WFC Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15454)
*Yotam Cohen*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文研究了哈勃太空望远镜ACS/WFC图像中因‘滚转漂移’（roll-drift）导致的未声明锁失事件对数据质量的影响，并通过模拟与现有数据处理技术量化其影响，提出一个可测量参数阈值，用于快速识别可能受滚转漂移影响的数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 2024年哈勃太空望远镜因运行变化出现未声明的锁失事件，导致曝光期间目标光斑模糊、数据退化甚至需重拍，亟需评估其影响并提供快速诊断方法。

Method: 利用模拟和现有数据处理技术，量化滚转漂移对ACS/WFC图像中可测量参数的影响，并确定一个判别阈值。

Result: 识别出一个关键可测量参数的阈值，当超过该阈值时，数据很可能受到滚转漂移影响，从而支持用户快速评估数据质量。

Conclusion: 该阈值为用户提供了简单有效的工具，以判断ACS/WFC数据是否需进一步检查或处理，提升了哈勃数据使用的可靠性与效率。

Abstract: In 2024, due to some operational changes, the Hubble Space Telescope began exhibiting undeclared loss of lock events. This loss of lock can result in the smearing out of light from the target field during an exposure, which leads to data degradation, which in turn may require data to be retaken. In this work, we investigate this `roll-drift' effect in ACS/WFC images. We quantify the impact of roll-drift on measurable parameters in data by using simulations and existing data reduction techniques. We identify a threshold of one such measurable parameter beyond which data may likely be affected by roll-drift, so that users can quickly and easily assess whether their data needs further attention.

</details>


### [131] [iDaVIE v1.0: A virtual reality tool for interactive analysis of astronomical data cubes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15490)
*Alexander Sivitilli,Lucia Marchetti,Angus Comrie,P. Cilliers Pretorius,Thijs,van der Hulst,Fabio Vitello,D. J. Pisano,Ugo Becciani,A. Russell Taylor,Paolo Serra,Mayhew Steyn,Michaela van Zyl*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文介绍了iDaVIE——一个面向天文学大数据的沉浸式虚拟现实（VR）数据可视化与交互探索平台，旨在提升多维天文数据的质量控制与科学解读效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代天文学面临前所未有的数据量，传统分析工具难以高效处理和直观理解高维数据；亟需能匹配复杂工作流、支持实时交互与质量控制的新型可视化工具。

Method: 基于Unity引擎与SteamVR开发开源VR软件套件iDaVIE，集成定制插件实现大数据立方体的高效解析、降采样与统计计算，并支持导入渲染、交互选择、裁剪、星表叠加及结果导出等功能。

Result: iDaVIE已成功应用于MeerKAT、ASKAP和APERTIF等望远镜的HI数据立方体验证、检测掩模优化与新源识别；显著降低高维数据认知负荷，提升科研效率。

Conclusion: iDaVIE作为可扩展、可协作、开源的沉浸式可视化平台，为天文大数据时代提供了创新的人机交互范式，有望推动自动化分析流程中人因环节的深度整合与效能跃升。

Abstract: As modern astronomy confronts unprecedented data volumes, automated pipelines and machine-learning techniques have become essential for processing and analysis. As these workflows grow more complex, astronomers also require input and inspection tools that can keep pace. To address challenges in navigating multidimensional datasets for quality control and scientific interpretation, we present the immersive Data Visualisation Interactive Explorer (iDaVIE), a virtual reality (VR) software suite developed in collaboration with the astronomy community. iDaVIE enables users to import and render large 3D data cubes within a VR environment, offering real-time tools for selection, cropping, catalogue overlays, and exporting results back into existing pipelines. Built on the Unity engine and SteamVR, the system uses custom plug-ins for efficient data parsing, downsampling, and statistical calculations. The software has already been integrated into workflows such as verifying HI data cubes from MeerKAT, ASKAP, and APERTIF, refining detection masks, and identifying new sources. Its intuitive interface aims to reduce the cognitive load associated with higher-dimensional data, allowing researchers to focus more directly on scientific goals. As an open-source, scalable, and adaptable platform, iDaVIE supports continued development and integration with other tools. Version 1.0 marks a significant milestone, with planned enhancements including subcube loading, advanced rendering modes, video-generation scripts, and collaborative capabilities. By pairing immersive visualisation with robust interaction tools, iDaVIE seeks to transform how researchers engage with complex datasets and enhance productivity in the era of big data.

### [132] [SIMTERFERE: An optical interferometry simulator for quantifying the coherent flux stability of VLTI/GRAVITY+. Reaching per mill stability: Application to exoplanet spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15499)
*J. R. Sauter,A. von Stauffenberg,G. Bourdarot,W. Brandner,F. Eisenhauer,L. Kreidberg,L. Labadie,S. Scheithauer,D. Trevascus,R. van Boekel*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文通过连续七小时观测恒星Beta Pictoris，评估GRAVITY+自适应光学系统的稳定性，并开发了数据驱动模拟工具SIMTERFERE来识别和校正仪器系统误差（如光纤耦合变化）及大气影响，最终实现0.1%精度的光子噪声极限校正，显著提升直接成像系外行星大气表征能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量化并表征GRAVITY+系统的短/长期稳定性，为未来系外行星观测提供基准。

Method: 对Beta Pictoris进行七小时连续观测；开发数据驱动模拟工具SIMTERFERE，结合仪器遥测数据复现观测；对比模拟与实测相干流量以溯源系统误差；采用多项式拟合和线性大气质量插值校正仪器与大气效应。

Result: 约10%的流量变化源于光纤耦合不稳定性，可用二阶多项式校正；剩余约1%变化主要为地气吸收，经对比谱法与大气质量插值可校正至0.1%精度（达光子噪声极限）。

Conclusion: GRAVITY+干涉仪具有极高稳定性，其低阶连续谱与地气变化均可高精度校正，使其成为直接成像系外行星高保真大气表征的独特利器。

Abstract: The implementation of the GRAVITY+ Adaptive Optics (GPAO) system at VLTI enables unprecedented sensitivity and stability in optical interferometry. This allows high-precision characterization of directly imaged exoplanets at medium spectral resolution, providing a new pathway for studying planetary atmospheres. We aim to quantify and characterize the short- and long-term stability of GRAVITY+ through a consecutive seven-hour observation of the bright and stable star beta Pictoris, providing a benchmark for future exoplanet observations. We developed SIMTERFERE, a data-driven simulation tool that reproduces GRAVITY+ on-star observations using ancillary instrument and telemetry data. By comparing the simulations with the measured coherent fluxes, we traced the origins of systematic flux variations and assessed their impact on exoplanet contrast measurements. We find that the approximately 10% variations are dominated by throughput changes driven by variable fiber coupling, which depends on wavefront stability, atmospheric dispersion, and residual fiber offsets. These variations appear as smooth continuum changes across wavelength and can be effectively mitigated using second-order polynomial corrections. After removing these instrumental effects, the remaining approximately 1% variations are almost purely of telluric origin, which we can reliably correct down to the photon-noise limit (0.1% precision) using a contrast spectrum approach with linear airmass interpolation. The GRAVITY+ inferometric instrument is highly stable: low-order continuum and telluric variations can be corrected with high precision, making it uniquely capable of high-fidelity characterization of directly imaged exoplanets.

</details>
